<div style="text-align:center"><div style="width:8.5in;text-align:left;margin-left: auto;margin-right: auto">
 <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold">Item&#160;2.02. &#160;Results of Operations and Financial Condition. </p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On January&#160;26, 2023, we issued the press release furnished as Exhibit 99.1. The press release describes the results of our operations for the quarter ended December&#160;31, 2022. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The information furnished in this Current Report on Form <span style="white-space:nowrap">8-K</span> under Item 2.02 and the attached exhibit shall not be deemed &#8220;filed&#8221; for purposes of Section&#160;18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended (the &#8220;Exchange Act&#8221;), or incorporated by reference in any filing under the Securities Act of 1933, as amended, or the Exchange Act, except as shall be expressly set forth by specific reference in such a filing. </p> <p style="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold">Item&#160;5.02. &#160;Departure of Directors or Certain Officers; Election of Directors; Appointment of Certain Officers; Compensatory Arrangements of Certain Officers. </p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On January&#160;25, 2023, our board of directors appointed Michael J. &#8220;Mick&#8221; Farrell as chair of our board of directors. Mick Farrell is our chief executive officer and a current director. The appointment was effective immediately. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Dr.&#160;Peter&#160;C. Farrell, our founder, who has served as chair of the board of directors since the company was founded in 1989, will continue as a director and as a <span style="white-space:nowrap">non-officer</span> employee of ResMed. In recognition of Dr.&#160;Farrell&#8217;s long and valuable service as chair, the board of directors appointed him to the new director position of chair emeritus, effective immediately. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Ron Taylor will continue to serve as our lead director. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">There are no compensation changes in connection with any of these appointments. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On January&#160;26, 2023, we issued the press release furnished as Exhibit 99.2. The press release announces the board position changes described above. </p> <p style="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold">Item&#160;8.01. &#160;Other Events. </p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On January&#160;26, 2023, we announced that our board of directors declared a quarterly cash dividend of US $0.44 per share. The dividend will have a record date of February&#160;9, 2023, payable on March&#160;16, 2023. The dividend will be paid in U.S. currency to holders of ResMed&#8217;s common stock trading on the New York Stock Exchange. Holders of CHESS Depositary Instruments trading on the Australian Securities Exchange will receive an equivalent amount in Australian currency, based on the exchange rate on the record date, and reflecting the 10:1 ratio between CDIs and NYSE shares. The <span style="white-space:nowrap">ex-dividend</span> date will be February&#160;8, 2023, for common stockholders and for CDI holders. ResMed has received a waiver from the ASX&#8217;s settlement operating rules, which will allow ResMed to defer processing conversions between its common stock and CDI registers from February&#160;8, 2023, through February&#160;9, 2023, inclusive. </p>
 <p style="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&#160;</p> <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:center">-2- </p>

</div></div>

</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>ResMed Inc. Announces Results for the Second Quarter of Fiscal Year 2023 </B></P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="9%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#150;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left"><I>Year-over-year revenue grows 16%, operating profit up 13%, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT>
operating profit up 14%</I> </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Note: A webcast of ResMed&#146;s conference call will be available at 4:30 p.m. ET today
at&nbsp;<U>http://investor.resmed.com</U> </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">SAN DIEGO, January&nbsp;26, 2023 &#150; ResMed Inc. (NYSE: RMD, ASX: RMD) today announced results for its
quarter ended December&nbsp;31, 2022. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Second Quarter 2023 Highlights </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>All comparisons are to the prior year period </I></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Revenue increased by 16% to $1,033.7&nbsp;million; up 20% on a constant currency basis</P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Gross margin contracted 30 bps to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">56.1%;&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;gross</FONT> margin
contracted 80 bps to 56.8% </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Income from operations increased <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">13%;&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;operating</FONT> profit
up 14% </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Diluted earnings per share of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">$1.53;&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;diluted</FONT> earnings
per share of $1.66 </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;During the second quarter, we significantly increased production and delivery of flow generator devices to
meet the incredible demand from customers, resulting in strong sales growth in the Americas, and solid overall performance for our business across 140 countries,&#148; said Mick Farrell, ResMed&#146;s CEO. &#147;Towards the end of the quarter, we
cleared the final regulatory hurdles and closed the acquisition of MEDIFOX DAN, expanding our outside-hospital
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Software-as-a-Service</FONT></FONT></FONT> (SaaS) business to its first market outside the U.S. We will deliver ongoing, sustainable growth through
this exciting expansion of our business model in Germany, with strong links to both our global SaaS business and our market-leading German business in sleep and respiratory care. Looking ahead, we remain focused on delivering lifesaving therapy
solutions and accelerating the adoption of digital health in sleep apnea, COPD, and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">out-of-hospital</FONT></FONT> care. During calendar year 2022, we improved over 149&nbsp;million
lives, and we are well on our way to our goal of helping 250&nbsp;million people sleep better, breathe better, and live higher-quality lives with outside-hospital care in 2025.&#148; </P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">In order to provide a framework for assessing how our underlying businesses performed excluding the effect of
foreign currency fluctuations, we provide certain financial information on a &#147;constant currency&#148; basis, which is in addition to the actual financial information presented. In order to calculate our constant currency information, we
translate the current period financial information using the foreign currency exchange rates that were in effect during the previous comparable period. However, constant currency measures should not be considered in isolation or as an alternative to
U.S. dollar measures that reflect current period exchange rates, or to other financial measures calculated and presented in accordance with U.S. GAAP. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

the end of the press release. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Discussion of Second Quarter Results </I></B></P>

STYLE="white-space:nowrap">$1.53.&nbsp;Non-GAAP&nbsp;net</FONT> income increased by 13% to $244.4&nbsp;million, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">and&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;diluted</FONT> earnings per share increased by 13% to $1.66, predominantly

capital. During the quarter we paid $64.5&nbsp;million in dividends. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Other Business and Operational Highlights </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Completed the acquisition of MEDIFOX DAN, a German leader in software solutions for <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">out-of-hospital</FONT></FONT> care providers. Similar to the solutions of ResMed&#146;s leading U.S. SaaS brands, Brightree and MatrixCare, MEDIFOX DAN expands ResMed&#146;s <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">out-of-hospital</FONT></FONT> SaaS business into new health sectors and builds on its established healthcare business in Germany. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Celebrated the grand opening of ResMed&#146;s new Advanced Manufacturing Centre in Tuas, Singapore. The <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">270,000-square-foot</FONT> <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">(25,000-square-meter)</FONT> facility more than doubles the size of ResMed&#146;s footprint in Singapore and serves as ResMed&#146;s key manufacturing hub in
Asia-Pacific. The facility has the manufacturing capacity and footprint to scale production for connected devices and mask systems to help people sleep, breathe, and live better lives. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Dividend program </I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The ResMed board of directors
today declared a quarterly cash dividend of $0.44 per share. The dividend will have a record date of February&nbsp;9, 2023, payable on March&nbsp;16, 2023. The dividend will be paid in U.S. currency to holders of ResMed&#146;s common stock trading
on the New York Stock Exchange. Holders of CHESS Depositary Interests (&#147;CDIs&#148;) trading on the Australian Securities Exchange will receive an equivalent amount in Australian currency, based on the exchange rate on the record date, and
reflecting the 10:1 ratio between CDIs and NYSE shares. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">The&nbsp;ex-dividend&nbsp;date</FONT> will be February&nbsp;8, 2023, for common stockholders and for CDI holders. ResMed has received a waiver from the
ASX&#146;s settlement operating rules, which will allow ResMed to defer processing conversions between its common stock and CDI registers from February&nbsp;8, 2023, through February&nbsp;9, 2023, inclusive.</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Webcast details </I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">ResMed will discuss its
second-quarter fiscal year 2023 results on its webcast at 1:30 p.m. U.S. Pacific Time today. The live webcast of the call can be accessed on ResMed&#146;s Investor Relations website at <U>investor.resmed.com</U>. Please go to this section of the
website and click on the icon for the &#147;Q2 2023 Earnings Webcast&#148; to register and listen to the live webcast. A replay of the earnings webcast will be accessible on the website and available approximately two hours after the live webcast.
In addition, a telephone replay of the conference call will be available approximately two hours after the webcast by dialing <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">+1&nbsp;877-660-6853&nbsp;(U.S.)</FONT></FONT> or <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">+1&nbsp;201-612-7415&nbsp;(outside</FONT></FONT> U.S.) and entering the passcode 13735371. The telephone replay will be available until February&nbsp;9, 2023. </P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>About ResMed </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">At ResMed (NYSE: RMD, ASX: RMD) we pioneer innovative solutions that treat and keep people out of the hospital, empowering them to live healthier,
higher-quality lives. Our digital health technologies and cloud-connected medical devices transform care for people with sleep apnea, COPD, and other chronic diseases. Our
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">comprehensive&nbsp;out-of-hospital&nbsp;software</FONT></FONT> platforms support the professionals and caregivers who help people stay healthy in the home or care setting of their
choice. By enabling better care, we improve quality of life, reduce the impact of chronic disease, and lower costs for consumers and healthcare systems in more than 140 countries.&nbsp;To learn more, visit <U>ResMed.com</U>&nbsp;and follow @ResMed.
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Safe harbor statement </I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Statements contained
in this release that are not historical facts are &#147;forward-looking&#148; statements as contemplated by the Private Securities Litigation Reform Act of 1995. These forward-looking statements &#150; including statements regarding ResMed&#146;s
projections of future revenue or earnings, expenses, new product development, new product launches, new markets for its products, the integration of acquisitions, litigation, and tax outlook &#150; are subject to risks and uncertainties, which could
cause actual results to materially differ from those projected or implied in the forward-looking statements. Additional risks and uncertainties are discussed in ResMed&#146;s periodic reports on file with the U.S. Securities&nbsp;&amp; Exchange
Commission. ResMed does not undertake to update its forward-looking statements. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">&#150; More &#150; </P>

<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(A)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">ResMed adjusts for the impact of the amortization of acquired intangibles, acquisition related expenses and the
reserve for disputed tax positions from their evaluation of ongoing operations, and believes that investors benefit from adjusting these items to facilitate a more meaningful evaluation of current operating performance. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">ResMed believes <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">that&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;diluted</FONT> earnings per share is an additional measure of
performance that investors can use to compare operating results between reporting periods. ResMed <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">uses&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;information</FONT> internally in planning, forecasting, and evaluating the results of
operations in the current period and in comparing it to past periods. ResMed believes this information provides investors better insight when evaluating ResMed&#146;s performance from core operations and provides consistent financial reporting. The
use <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">of&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;measures</FONT> is intended to supplement, and not to replace, the presentation of net income and other GAAP measures. Like
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">all&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;measures,&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;earnings</FONT></FONT> are subject to inherent limitations because they do not include all the expenses that must be included under
GAAP. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">&#150; More &#150; </P>
</DIV></Center>

foreign currency fluctuations, we provide certain financial information on a &#147;constant currency basis,&#148; which is in addition to the actual financial information presented. In order to calculate our constant currency information, we
translate the current period financial information using the foreign currency exchange rates that were in effect during the previous comparable period. However, constant currency measures should not be considered in isolation or as an alternative to
U.S. dollar measures that reflect current period exchange rates, or to other financial measures calculated and presented in accordance with U.S. GAAP. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 99.2 </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>ResMed appoints Michael Farrell as Chair of its Board of Directors </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Peter Farrell to become Chair Emeritus </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>SAN DIEGO, January</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;26, 2023</B> &#150; ResMed (NYSE: RMD, ASX: RMD) today announced ResMed&#146;s board of directors has appointed chief
executive officer Michael (&#147;Mick&#148;) Farrell as chair of the board, effective January&nbsp;25, 2023. Mr.&nbsp;Farrell succeeds current chair Peter Farrell who will become chair emeritus and will remain an active board member. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Mick Farrell became ResMed&#146;s CEO on March&nbsp;1, 2013, and has served as a member of the company&#146;s board of directors since assuming that role.
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;I am honored to expand my role with ResMed as its next chair and to succeed my dad, Peter Farrell, whose vision, leadership, and guidance have
helped ResMed become the largest outside-hospital, digital health company in the world,&#148; said Mick Farrell. &#147;I look forward to working with and leading our strong, diverse, and talented board in continued value creation for stockholders
and all our stakeholders.&#148; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;I am grateful for the opportunities I have had to lead ResMed and its board over the past many years,&#148; said
Peter Farrell. &#147;ResMed is on a clear growth path with strategic priorities intact; it&#146;s the right time for me to step aside and reduce my commitments as chair so I can devote more time to other boards and philanthropic interests. I will
remain an active ResMed board member as chair emeritus and will continue to work closely with Mick, ResMed management, and the board as a steward of ResMed&#146;s strategy, innovation, and culture.&#148; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;I&#146;d like to thank Peter for his leadership and many contributions to ResMed over the years,&#148; said Ron Taylor, ResMed&#146;s lead independent
director and chair of the nominating and governance committee. &#147;We&#146;re pleased to welcome Mick to the board chair position. Over the past 10 years, the board and I have worked closely with and observed Mick in his role as director and as
CEO. Under Mick&#146;s leadership of ResMed these last 10 years, we have seen the market capitalization of the company grow from $6&nbsp;billion to over $30&nbsp;billion, delivering a total shareholder return of 507% or 20.0% average annual growth
in value over that same period; an excellent return for all our stakeholders. We believe Mick has the right skills and experience, and he has been effective in setting the board agenda, encouraging debate, and connecting the board with management
for many years. Combining the chair and CEO roles will allow for streamlining and efficiency and is aligned with the structure held by many of our peers on the S&amp;P 500.<SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP> I look forward to
working with Mick and the rest of the board as we support the company in reaching its goal of changing the lives of 250&nbsp;million people in 2025.&#148; </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><I><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP>&nbsp;</I></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left"><I>Over 40% of the S&amp;P 500 companies combine the chair and CEO roles, including 11 of the 14 other
healthcare equipment companies in the S&amp;P 500. </I></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>About ResMed </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">At ResMed (NYSE: RMD, ASX: RMD) we pioneer innovative solutions that treat and keep people out of the hospital, empowering them to live healthier,
higher-quality lives. Our digital health technologies and cloud-connected medical devices transform care for people with sleep apnea, COPD, and other chronic diseases. Our comprehensive
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">out-of-hospital</FONT></FONT> software platforms support the professionals and caregivers who help people stay healthy in the home or care setting of their choice. By enabling better
care, we improve quality of life, reduce the impact of chronic disease, and lower costs for consumers and healthcare systems in more than 140 countries.&nbsp;To learn more, visit <U>ResMed.com</U> and follow @ResMed. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"># # # </P>
</DIV></Center>
